string \textbf{ Format} (string \+\_\+\+String, string \+\_\+\+Format)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Returns string formatted by format parameter wich can assume special values as if start by 0 or \# will be formatted as common double value number format string; \&D,\&DATE for date format; \$,\&CUR for currency format; \&CURNZ for currency format, empty if zero; !,\&UPPER for uppercase format; \&HM for HH\+:MM time format; \&T, \&HMS, \&TIME for HH\+:\+MM\+:SS time format; \&DT, \&DATETIME form datetime format; \&DU, \&DURATION form duration format HHHHHH\+:\+MM\+:\+SS\+:ZZZ; \&DUS, \&DURATIONSEC form duration format HHHHHH\+:\+MM\+:SS; \&DUM, \&DURATIONMIN form duration format HHHHHH\+:MM; \&DUMNZ form duration format HHHHHH\+:MM or string empty if zero; \&DUC, \&DURATIONCENT form duration format HHHHHH.\+CC; \&DUD, \&DURATIONDAY form duration format DDDD.\+CC; \&LOWER for lowercase format; \&CUR+ for currency more accurate format; \&CUR+\+NZ for currency more accurate format, empty if zero; \&QTY for quantity format; \&QTYNZ form quantity format, empty if zero; \&QTY+ for quantity more accurate format; \&QTY+\+NZ form quantity more accurate format, empty if zero; \&EU,\&EUR,\&EURO for euro money format; \&EUNZ,\&EURNZ,\&EURONZ for euro money format with empty string if zero; \&USD,\&DOLLAR for US dollar money format; \&USDNZ,\&DOLLARNZ for US dollar money format with empty string if zero. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\doxyref{SMCode}{p.}{class_s_m_code_system_1_1_s_m_code} cache values management class. 

\doxyref{SMCode}{p.}{class_s_m_code_system_1_1_s_m_code} zip compression and decompression functions require third-\/party Dot\+Net\+Zip 1.\+16.\+0 Nu\+Get packet (Author\+: Henrik/\+Dino Chiesa).

\doxyref{SMCode}{p.}{class_s_m_code_system_1_1_s_m_code} application class\+: logger.

Web functions class.

Google services management functions.

\doxyref{SMCode}{p.}{class_s_m_code_system_1_1_s_m_code} application class\+: unique id.

\doxyref{SMCode}{p.}{class_s_m_code_system_1_1_s_m_code} application class\+: system.

\doxyref{SMCode}{p.}{class_s_m_code_system_1_1_s_m_code} application class\+: strings.

\doxyref{SMCode}{p.}{class_s_m_code_system_1_1_s_m_code} application class\+: sort.

\doxyref{SMCode}{p.}{class_s_m_code_system_1_1_s_m_code} application class\+: path.

\doxyref{SMCode}{p.}{class_s_m_code_system_1_1_s_m_code} application class\+: parser.

Returns string formatted by format parameter wich can assume special values as if start by 0 or \# will be formatted as common double value number format string; \&D,\&DATE for date format; \$,\&CUR for currency format; \&CURNZ for currency format, empty if zero; !,\&UPPER for uppercase format; \&HM for HH\+:MM time format; \&T, \&HMS, \&TIME for HH\+:\+MM\+:SS time format; \&DT, \&DATETIME form datetime format; \&DU, \&DURATION form duration format HHHHHH\+:\+MM\+:\+SS\+:ZZZ; \&DUS, \&DURATIONSEC form duration format HHHHHH\+:\+MM\+:SS; \&DUM, \&DURATIONMIN form duration format HHHHHH\+:MM; \&DUMNZ form duration format HHHHHH\+:MM or string empty if zero; \&DUC, \&DURATIONCENT form duration format HHHHHH.\+CC; \&DUD, \&DURATIONDAY form duration format DDDD.\+CC; \&LOWER for lowercase format; \&CUR+ for currency more accurate format; \&CUR+\+NZ for currency more accurate format, empty if zero; \&QTY for quantity format; \&QTYNZ form quantity format, empty if zero; \&QTY+ for quantity more accurate format; \&QTY+\+NZ form quantity more accurate format, empty if zero; \&EU,\&EUR,\&EURO for euro money format; \&EUNZ,\&EURNZ,\&EURONZ for euro money format with empty string if zero; \&USD,\&DOLLAR for US dollar money format; \&USDNZ,\&DOLLARNZ for US dollar money format with empty string if zero.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_s_m_code_system_1_1_s_m_code_aa42415e685360bf3ba85d8045f6f2fad}

Returns a string with current OS version description as\+: 95, 98, 98SE ME, NT, 2000, XP, VISTA, WINDOWS7, WINDOWS8, WINDOWS10 or empty string if fails. To let function work properly add application manifest file and remove remarks on windows 8 and windows 10 compatibility items.
